<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/1992513/djy/blob/master/gb/24/8/14/n14311365.md#1" target="_blank">加州学校9项新法迎新生</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/1992513/djy/blob/master/gb/24/8/14/n14311365.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2024/08/id14311369-Chargers-Dairy-School-Event-3_JF_11152022-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>全加州各地的K-12学校开学在即，立法者们已通过了如下九项新法律，旨在让教育体验更加安全、健康和包容。

“剧透”：立法者并未取消突袭测验。
1. 休息时间规定
